Bot : api_call:request_account_api
API : api_response:request_accounts_api, list_of_accounts:Checkin,Credit,Savings
Bot : You have the following accounts : Checkin,Credit,Savings , which one do you wish ?
User : use Credit
Bot : api_call:check_account_api, user_account:Credit
API : api_response api_response:account_check_api, api_result:success
Bot : api_call:check_balance_api, user_account:Credit
API : api_response api_response:account_balance_api, api_result:success, balance:400
Bot : end_call your current balance for account is 400
